<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=ESL/Meisterschaft/2020/Season_2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b></li>
<li><b>Group Stage</b> - <i>September 22nd - November 24th, 2020</i>
<ul><li>Two groups of six teams each</li>
<li>Double round-robin</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-two">Bo2</abbr>
<ul><li>Teams earn 3 points per game win</li></ul></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">Top team</span> from each group advance to the playoffs semifinals</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(229,244,198);">2<sup>nd</sup> and 3<sup>rd</sup> place teams</span> from each group advance to the playoffs quarterfinals</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(249,222,199);">4<sup>th</sup> place teams</span> from each group are eliminated but invited for next season</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Bottom two teams</span> from each group are eliminated and drop down to relegation playoffs</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Playoffs</b>
<ul><li>Single-elimination bracket</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Broadcast_Talent">Broadcast Talent</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=ESL/Meisterschaft/2020/Season_2&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Broadcast Talent">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
